<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:universum.html>universum</a> (3439)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:universum.html>universum</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a>, as a whole, the universe</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>, neuter of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">universus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all together, whole, entire, collective, general, literally <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> or combined into one</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">uni-</i>, combining form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">unus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">versus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">verto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***unter.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> (98191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">under</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">untar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*under</i> (compare Old Saxon <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">undar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hunsrik" class="extiw" title="w:Hunsrik">Hunsrik</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hrx">unne</i>, Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i>, English <i>under</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>under</li>
<li>below</li>
<li>among, between
<ul><li><b>1919</b>, Walther <a href = vnd.unilang:kabel.html>Kabel</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/de:Irrende_Seelen" class="extiw" title="s:de:Irrende Seelen">Irrende Seelen</a></i>, Werner Dietsch Verlag, page 108:
<dl><dd>Unsere Unterredung wurde <a href = vnd.unilang:jetzt.html>jetzt</a> im leichten Plauderton geführt <a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a> ein harmloses Gespräch <b><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:guten.html>guten</a> Bekannten.
<dl><dd>Our discussion <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> now <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> in a light conversational tone like a harmless chat between friendly acquaintances.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> with; along with; accompanied by an action (often concessive)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> englische Sprache überlebte <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> normannische Eroberung <b><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></b> weitgehendem Verlust ihrer ursprünglichen Struktur.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The English language survived the <a href = vnd.unilang:norman.html>Norman</a> conquest, largely losing, however, its original structure.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> or regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> during</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The preposition <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used with accusative case if the verb indicates movement from one place to another, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used with dative case if the verb indicates location.</li>
<li>The sense “during” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> chiefly restricted to a few expressions, such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Woche</i> (“during the week, on weekdays”), in standard usage. In southern German speech it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used more freely.</li>
<li>With a definite article, the following contractions may occur: <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unterm</i> (= <a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> <span class="Latn" lang="de">dem</span>), <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">untern</i> (= <a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> <span class="Latn" lang="de">den</span>), and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">unters</i> (= <a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a> <span class="Latn" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:das.html>das</a></span>). These are non-obligatory contractions.</li></ul>
</body>

***updaten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:updaten.html>updaten</a> (58820)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">update</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:updaten.html>updaten</a></strong>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The singular form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> normally used after numerals. Thus: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vele.html>vele</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uren.html>uren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></i> – for many <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a>; but: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>lang</a></i> – for three <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">urewerc</i>. ***uw.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> (119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*iuwa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*izweraz</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jouw.html>jouw</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive,independent possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uwe.html>uwe</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>Second-person singular and plural</i>; your</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In standard Dutch this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the polite form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jouw.html>jouw</a></i>. However, in Flanders it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> commonly used as both formal and informal. The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jouw.html>jouw</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not commonly used in Flanders. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>Uw</a></i> may merge  with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i> in some dialects and sociolects.
</p>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a> (512)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vake</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">often</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">faka</i>, dative singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">compartment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vak.html>vak</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vaak</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaker.html>vaker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vaakst</b>)

<p>From the adverb.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaak.html>vake</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">facon</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaal.html>vaal</a> (55647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vāle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*falo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*falu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*falwaz</i>
</p>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of skin</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sallow, pallid</li>

***vaardig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaardig.html>vaardig</a> (24011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vardich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verdich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vaerdich</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaart.html>vaart</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>. Originally, the word meant "ready for departure".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaardig.html>vaardig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaardig.html>vaardiger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vaardigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>skillful</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ready</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaccin.html>vaccin</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vaccīnus</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vacca</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (because of early use of the cowpox virus against smallpox). Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">variola vaccīna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cowpox</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vacht.html>vacht</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fahtiz</i>. Related to Old Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head hair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vas.html>vas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">head hair</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***vader.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a> (157)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vāder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fadar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fadēr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ph₂tḗr</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vaders.html>vaders</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">gevaderen</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vadertje.html>vadertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>father
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Luuk, <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Luuk, I am your <b>father</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>forefather
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beschrijft.html>beschrijft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daden.html>daden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vaderen.html>vaderen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This books describes the doings of our <b>forefathers</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fāgen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*fēgijaną</i>. A variant form with <a href = vnd.unilang:umlaut.html>umlaut</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> rise to modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vegen.html>vegen</a></i>.

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vagen.html>vagen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sweep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vuur.html>vuur</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vac</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fak</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*faką</i>. In some of the contemporary senses probably influenced by cognate <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Fach</i>.
